During the Spring Festival, Ximen is not allowed to drive up the mountain. You can take a shuttle bus. It costs about 115 for adults including the ticket. The ticket can be entered and exited in 2 days. There is an elevator to the top of the mountain. You don‚Äôt have to walk much. It is less crowded and more cost-effective than taking the cable car at the east gate.
Facilities: The facilities of the old star-rated hotel are still good, but they are a bit old. There is a lot of moldy wood in the shower room in the hot spring area, and the toilet also smells. However, it is good to provide a dehydrator service for dehydrating swimsuits. Hot springs are divided into indoor and outdoor ones. Outdoor hot springs have different feelings during the day and night. If you want to see the beautiful scenery, it is recommended to go to the infinity hot spring pool during the day.
There are quite a lot of varieties for breakfast. I had some pig-killing noodles, which was goodüëç
